///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_Vessel
//
//	Inherite from CDB_Product
//
//	new:CDB_Vessel(ID)->tableID
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					0				isDeleted
//					1				isAvailable
//					0				isHidden
//					1				isFix
//					0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//					0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      			0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//				}
//				Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//				PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//				Tmax in �C
//				Tmin in �C
//			}
//			"Reference"				Reference to the Product
//			"Name"					Name of the product
//			TypeID					Identifier of the product type
//			FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//			VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//			PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//			Comment					Product comment
//			ProdImgID				Product image ID
//			AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//			PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//			TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//			Price					Price of the product
// 			ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//			AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//			isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   		AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//			AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//		}
//		NominalVolume		double (m3)
//		FactoryP0			double (Pa)
//		ConnectID			string ID
//		SizeID				string ID
//		Height				double (m)
//		Diameter			double (m)
//		Weight				double (kg)
// 		FloorStanding 		can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
// 		Compatibilityflags  can be combined #ePMComp_Statico | #ePMComp_Compresso | #ePMComp_Transfero | #ePMComp_TransferoTI | ePMComp_VsslIntCoating
//		SecondaryVesselID	Identifier of the associated secondary vessel
//		PlenoID				Identifier of the Pleno group that match the vessel.
//      PSch                SWKI 93-1: Pressure up to which the expansion vessel must not subject to authorization, according to Swiss directive SICC 93-1.
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//	CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//
//	CDB_Vessel::NominalVolume
//	CDB_Vessel::FactoryP0
//	CDB_Vessel::ConnectID
//	CDB_Vessel::SizeID
//	CDB_Vessel::Height
//	CDB_Vessel::Diameter
//	CDB_Vessel::Weight
//	CDB_Vessel::InstallationLayout
//	CDB_Vessel::CompatibilityFlags
//	CDB_Vessel::SecVsslID
//	CDB_Vessel::PlenoID
//  CDB_Vessel::PSch
// }

//****************************
// STATICO SD
//****************************

new:CDB_Vessel(STAT_SD8_3) -> VSSL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0											// isDeleted
				1											// isAvailable
				0											// isHidden
				1											// isFix
				0											// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
				0											// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               							// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			3.0e+5 \ 3.0e+5								// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax  in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID										// Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			70.0	        							// Tmax in �C
			5.0             							// Tmin in �C
		}
		"710 1000"									// Reference to the Product
		"SD 8.3"									// Name of the product
		VSSLTYPE_STAT								// Identifier of the product type
		VSSLFAM_SD									// Identifier of the family of the product
		VERS_VSLSTD									// Identifier of the version of the product
		1											// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""											// Product comment
		"PX_STATICO_SD"		//TODO 					// Product image ID
		ACCVSSLGR_SD_8_12							// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo 								// Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
		NO_ID										// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0											// Price
		#eProduct                       			// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                               			// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
	}
	8.0e-3										// NominalVolume
	1.0e+5										// FactoryP0
	CONN_THR_M_R								// ConnectID
	DN_15										// SizeID
	1.66e-1										// Height
	3.14e-1										// Diameter
	3.5											// Weight
	#eWallHanged								// FloorStanding: can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
	#ePMComp_Statico							// Compatibilityflags: can be combined #ePMComp_Statico | #ePMComp_Compresso | #ePMComp_Transfero | #ePMComp_TransferoTI | ePMComp_VsslIntCoating
	NO_ID										// Identifier of the associated secondary vessel
	PLENOGROUP_STATICO							// Identifier of the Pleno group that match the vessel.
	0.0											// PSch: not used in this case.
	0											// Accept Tecbox on top: 0/1.
}

	{
		{
			{
				0											// isDeleted
				1											// isAvailable
				0											// isHidden
				1											// isFix
				0											// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
				0											// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               							// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			2.5e+6 \ 2.5e+6								// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax  in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID										// Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			70.0	        							// Tmax in �C
			5.0             							// Tmin in �C
		}
		"301012 01300"								// Reference to the Product
		"SH 150.25"									// Name of the product
		VSSLTYPE_STAT								// Identifier of the product type
		VSSLFAM_SH									// Identifier of the family of the product
		VERS_VSLSTD									// Identifier of the version of the product
		1											// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""											// Product comment
		"PX_STATICO_SH"			 					// Product image ID
		ACCVSSLGR_SH								// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo 								// Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
		NO_ID										// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0											// Price
		#eProduct                       			// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                               			// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
	}
	0.15										// NominalVolume
	4.0e+5										// FactoryP0
	CONN_THR_M_R								// ConnectID
	DN_32										// SizeID
	1.07										// Height
	0.5											// Diameter
	71											// Weight
	#eFloorStanding								// FloorStanding: can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
	#ePMComp_Transfero							// Compatibilityflags: can be combined #ePMComp_Statico | #ePMComp_Compresso | #ePMComp_Transfero | #ePMComp_TransferoTI
	NO_ID										// Identifier of the associated secondary vessel
	NO_ID										// Identifier of the Pleno group that match the vessel.
	0.0											// PSch: not used in this case.
	0											// Accept Tecbox on top: 0/1.
}

//****************************
// Simply Compresso - Primary integrated vessel
//****************************
new:CDB_Vessel(COMPR_CD80_9) -> VSSL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0											// isDeleted
				1											// isAvailable
				0											// isHidden
				1											// isFix
				0											// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
				0											// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               							// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			9.0e+5 \ 9.0e+5								// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax  in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID										// Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			70.0	        							// Tmax in �C
			5.0             							// Tmin in �C
		}
		"-"				// No reference, this vessel is built-in in the Simply Compresso and can't be bought separately
		"CD 80.9"									// Name of the product
		VSSLTYPE_PRIM								// Identifier of the product type
		VSSLFAM_CD									// Identifier of the family of the product
		VERS_VSLSTD									// Identifier of the version of the product
		1											// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""											// Product comment
		"NO_ID"										// Product image ID
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo 								// Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
		NO_ID										// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0											// Price
		#eProduct                       			// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                               			// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
	}
	0.08										// NominalVolume
	0											// FactoryP0
	CONN_THR_M_R								// ConnectID
	DN_20										// SizeID
	0.346										// Height
	0.636										// Diameter
	16											// Weight
	#eIntegrated								// FloorStanding: can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
	#ePMComp_Compresso							// Compatibilityflags: can be combined #ePMComp_Statico | #ePMComp_Compresso | #ePMComp_Transfero | #ePMComp_TransferoTI
	COMPR_CD80_9E								// Identifier of the associated secondary vessel
	PLENOGROUP_CONNECT							// Identifier of the Pleno group that match the vessel.
	3.75e+5										// PSch: not used in this case.
	0											// Accept Tecbox on top: 0/1.
}

new:CDB_Vessel(AQUA_AD8_10) -> VSSL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0											// isDeleted
				1											// isAvailable
				0											// isHidden
				1											// isFix
				0											// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
				0											// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               							// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			1.0e+6 \ 1.0e+6								// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax  in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID										// Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			70.0	        							// Tmax in �C
			5.0             							// Tmin in �C
		}
		"711 1000"									// Reference to the Product
		"AD 8.10"									// Name of the product
		VSSLTYPE_AQUA								// Identifier of the product type
		VSSLFAM_AD									// Identifier of the family of the product
		VERS_VSLSTD									// Identifier of the version of the product
		1											// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""											// Product comment
		"NO_ID"	 									// Product image ID
		NO_ID		//TODO							// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo 								// PartOfaSet			Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
		NO_ID										// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0											// Price
		#eProduct                       			// #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                               			// 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                           			// Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID										// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth			
	}
	8.0e-3										// NominalVolume (m3)
	4.0e+5										// FactoryP0 (Pa)
	CONN_THR_M_R								// ConnectID
	DN_15										// SizeID
	1.66e-1										// Height (m)
	3.14e-1										// Diameter (m)
	3.8											// Weight (kg)
	#eWallHanged								// FloorStanding: can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
	#ePMComp_Statico							// Compatibilityflags: can be combined #ePMComp_Statico | #ePMComp_Compresso | #ePMComp_Transfero | #ePMComp_TransferoTI
	NO_ID										// Identifier of the associated secondary vessel
	NO_ID										// Identifier of the Pleno group that match the vessel.
	0.0											// PSch: not used in this case.
	0											// Accept Tecbox on top: 0/1.
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table VSSLACCGROUP_TAB : Vessel accessory groups
//
//		Rules:
//			ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID	// ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//			ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID	// ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//			>ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is built-in
//			^ACXXXID			// ACXXXID excludes all others
//		  	*ACXXXID			// ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			#ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//			+ACXXXID 			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//			++ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// TODO: ACCGR for SG vessels and large MN vessels
// TODO: ACCGR for secondary and intermediate vessels to be set to NO_ID ???

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCVSSLGR_SD_8_12) -> VSSLACCGROUP_TAB
{
	{
		"Statico SD 8 & 12"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}
	#LSV_DLV_15
	ACCPM_H \ !ACCPM_TH
	ACCPM_TH \ !ACCPM_H
	ACCPM_DH15
}

//
//								CDB_TBCurve
//
//	Inherite from CDB_Curve
//
//	new:CDB_TBCurve(ID)->tableID
//	{
//		{
//			n				// Number of functions associated to the abscissa.
//			x0 \ y0			// Points X0\Y0(0)\...\Y0(n-1)
//			x1 \ y1
//			...
//		}
//		qNmin \ qNmax		// Min \ Max equalizing flow
//		Pmin \ Pmax			// Min \ Max Target pressure min \ max
//		CurveName			// Curve name
//	}
//CDB_TBCurve::qNminqNmax
//CDB_TBCurve::PminPmax
//CDB_TBCurve::CurveNameIDS

///////////////////////////////////////////
// From the Pneumatex equation, we transform to adapt to SI units.
// And in HySelect we use the curve with pman instead of p0.
// p0 = -150*qN^(-1)+60*(qN)^(-0,29)-5,5-(qN/1000)^2/25^2										qN[l/h]  p0[bar]
// p0 = (-150*(qN*3,6e6)^(-1)+60*(qN*3,6e6)^(-0,29)-5,5-(qN*3600,0)^2/25^2)*100000				qN[m3/s] p0[Pa]
// pman = (-150*(qN*3,6e6)^(-1)+60*(qN*3,6e6)^(-0,29)-5,5-(qN*3600,0)^2/25^2+0,4)*100000		qN[m3/s] pman[Pa]
///////////////////////////////////////////
// C 10.1 Connect compressor
new:CDB_TBCurve(TBC_CMPRS_C_10_1_CON)->TBPUMPCOMPRESSCURVE_TAB
{
	{
		1						// Number of functions associated to the abscissa.
		9.88888888889E-05 \ 5.40e5				// The computed value is "5.39865289484E+05" but we want here to match the fixed limit defined below for target pressure max.
		2.19611111111E-04 \ 3.37377597835E+05
		3.40333333333E-04 \ 2.40598948001E+05
		4.61055555556E-04 \ 1.79293310004E+05
		5.81777777778E-04 \ 1.35332866293E+05
		7.02500000000E-04 \ 1.01483357497E+05
	}
	9.88888888889E-05 \ 7.02500000000E-04   	// Min \ Max equalizing flow
	4.e4 \ 5.40e5								// Min \ Max Target pressure min \ max
	"C 10.1 Connect"							// Curve name
}

//
//								CDB_TecBox	// Transfero // Compresso
//
//	Inherite from CDB_Product
//
//	new:CDB_TecBox(ID)->tableID
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					0				isDeleted
//					1				isAvailable
//					0				isHidden
//					1				isFix
//					0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//					0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      			0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//				}
//				Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//				PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//				Tmax in �C
//				Tmin in �C
//			}
//			"Reference"				Reference to the Product
//			"Name"					Name of the product
//			TypeID					Identifier of the product type
//			FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//			VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//			PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//			Comment					Product comment
//			ProdImgID				Product image ID
//			AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//			PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//			TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//			Price					Price of the product
// 			ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//			AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//			isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   		AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//			AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//		}
//		IPxx					Enclosure protection
//		Power supply			List of accepted Power supplies separated by \
//		Frequency				Accepted frequency
//		Power					Power consumption
//		SoundPressureLevel		Sound pressure level only for compresso and vento
//		NbrPumpCompressor		0/1/2 ( 0 for CX )
//		PumpCompressCurveID 	Pumpt/Compressor curve ID
//		Accuracy				in Pascal
//		InstallationLayout		Can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
//		Height					double (m)
//		Width					double (m)
//		Depth					double (m)
//		Weight					double (kg)
// 		Functions 				#ePMFunc_None, #ePMFunc_Degasing, #ePMFunc_WaterMakeUp, #ePMFunc_Compressor or #ePMFunc_Pump should be a geometric progression 1,2,4,8,...
// 		FunctionsExclusion 		#ePMFunc_None, #ePMFunc_Degasing, #ePMFunc_WaterMakeUp, #ePMFunc_Compressor or #ePMFunc_Pump should be a geometric progression 1,2,4,8,...
// 		TecBox Variant			#ePMVariant_None/#ePMVariant_Cooling/#ePMVariant_EcoAuto/#ePMVariant_BreakTank/#ePMVariant_IntBufferVssl
//		TmaxWaterMakeUp			Max admissible temperature for WM (~30�C)
//		PlenoID					Identifier of the Pleno group that match the tecbox.
//		IntegratedVesselID		Identifier of the buffer vessel ID if fixed for Transfero or integrated vessel ID if fixed for Simply Compresso
//      WaterTreatmentCombID	Identifier of the different combination of the water treatment.
//      MaxSecondaryVessels		Maximum allowed secondary vessel. If -1 we take the 'm_iMaxNumberOfVesselsInParallel' - 1 from the technical parameters.
//
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//	CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//
//  CDB_TecBox::IPxx
//  CDB_TecBox::PowerSupplyIDs
//  CDB_TecBox::FrequencyID
//  CDB_TecBox::Power
//  CDB_TecBox::SoundPressureLevel
//  CDB_TecBox::NbrPumpCompressor
//  CDB_TecBox::PumpCompressCurveID
//  CDB_TecBox::Accuracy
//  CDB_TecBox::InstallationLayout
//  CDB_TecBox::Height
//  CDB_TecBox::Width
//  CDB_TecBox::Depth
//  CDB_TecBox::Weight
//  CDB_TecBox::Functions
//  CDB_TecBox::FunctionsExclusion
//  CDB_TecBox::TecBoxVariant
//  CDB_TecBox::TmaxWaterMakeUp
//  CDB_TecBox::PlenoID
//  CDB_TecBox::IntegratedVesselID
//  CDB_TecBox::WaterTreatmentCombID
//  CDB_TecBox::MaxSecondaryVessels

				0               										// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).

		TBXFAM_TRANSFERO_TV_C									// Identifier of the family of the product

	60														// Sound pressure level only for compresso and vento

	TBC_PUMP_TVC_4_1E										// PumpCompressCurveID
	2e+4													// Accuracy in Pascal
	#eFloorStanding											// InstallationLayout: can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated

	#ePMFunc_None											// Functions exclusion: #ePMFunc_None, #ePMFunc_Degasing, #ePMFunc_WaterMakeUp, #ePMFunc_Compressor or #ePMFunc_Pump geometric progression 1,2,4,8,...
	#ePMVariant_EcoAuto | #ePMVariant_VacuumDegassing		// TecBox Variant: #ePMVariant_None/#ePMVariant_Cooling/#ePMVariant_EcoAuto/#ePMVariant_BreakTank/#ePMVariant_VacuumDegassing/#ePMVariant_ExternalAir/#ePMVariant_IntBufferVssl/#ePMVariant_HighFlowTemp/#ePMVariant_IntegratedPrimaryVessel

	PMBUFVSL_TV_4_6_8									    // Identifier of the integrated vessel ID (type of integrated vessel is defined in the TecBox variant)

	-1														// Maximum allowed secondary vessel. If -1 we take the 'm_iMaxNumberOfVesselsInParallel' - 1 from the technical parameters.

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_TBPlenoVento
//
//	Inherited from CDB_TecBox
//
//	new:CDB_TBPlenoVento(ID)->tableID
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					{
//						0				isDeleted
//						1				isAvailable
//						0				isHidden
//						1				isFix
//						0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//						0				Free integer
//      				0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//					}
//					Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//					PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//					Tmax in �C
//					Tmin in �C
//				}
//				"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//				"Name"					Name of the product
//				TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//				FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//				VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//				PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//				Comment					Product comment
//				ProdImgID				Product image ID
//				AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//				PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//				TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//				Price					Price of the product
// 				ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//				AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//				isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   			AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//				AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//			}
//			IPxx					Enclosure protection
//			Power supply			List of accepted Power supplies separated by "\"
//			Frequency				Accepted frequency
//			Power					Power consumption
//			SoundPressureLevel		Sound pressure level only for compresso and vento
//			NbrPumpCompressor		0/1/2 ( 0 for CX )
//			PumpCompressCurveID		Pump/compressor curve ID.
//			Accuracy				in Pascal
//			InstallationLayout		Can be #eWallHanged, #eFloorStanding, #eFloorStandingNextTo, #eFloorStandingInFront, #eVesselTop or #eIntegrated
//			Height					double (m)
//			Width					double (m)
//			Depth					double (m)
//			Weight					double (kg)
//			Functions 				#ePMFunc_None, #ePMFunc_Degasing, #ePMFunc_WaterMakeUp, #ePMFunc_Compressor or #ePMFunc_Pump should be a geometric progression 1,2,4,8,...
// 			Functions exclusion		#ePMFunc_None, #ePMFunc_Degasing, #ePMFunc_WaterMakeUp, #ePMFunc_Compressor or #ePMFunc_Pump geometric progression 1,2,4,8,...
// 			TecBox Variant			#ePMVariant_None/#ePMVariant_Cooling/#ePMVariant_EcoAuto/#ePMVariant_BreakTank/#ePMVariant_VacuumDegassing/
//									#ePMVariant_ExternalAir/#ePMVariant_IntBufferVssl/#ePMVariant_HighFlowTemp
//			TmaxWaterMakeUp			Max admissible temperature for WM (~30�C)
//			PlenoID					Identifier of the Pleno group that match the Transfero/Compresso TecBox.
//			IntegratedVesselID		Identifier of the buffer vessel ID if fixed for Transfero or integrated vessel ID if fixed for Simply Compresso.
//     	 	WaterTreatmentCombID	Identifier of the different combination of the water treatment.
//      	MaxSecondaryVessels		Maximum allowed secondary vessel. If -1 we take the 'm_iMaxNumberOfVesselsInParallel' - 1 from the technical parameters.
//		}
//		SystemVolume										double (m3) for CPV,TV,...
//		WorkingPressRangeMin \ WorkingPressRangeMax			double Dpp for Pleno
//		FlowWaterMakeUp										double (VNS in DE)
//		Kvs													double (Pleno P, Pi)
//		Refillable					#ePMPR_RefillNone/#ePMPR_RefillOptional/#ePMPR_RefillMandatory
//		RefillGroupID				Identifier of the Pleno Refill group that match the Pleno.
//      MinimumVesselVolume			Identify what is the minimum vessel volume allowed with this Vento (See DataBObj.h for more details).
//	}
//
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table PLENOREFILLCOMB_TAB : Pleno Refill combinations
//
// It's a special use of 'CTableSet' and 'CDB_Set' for the pressurisation maintenance.
// With TV Connect we can have different configuration of Pleno and Refill.
// Each configuration is defined by a 'CDB_Set'.
//
//	new:CDB_Set(ID)
//	{
//		--> CDB_Thing
//		"Reference"			Reference to the TA Product
//		"Name"				Name of the product
//		CVID				Identifier of the control valve
//		ACTID				Identifier of the actuator
//		AccessGroupID		Identifier of the accessory group
//      "Parameter"			String to allow to apply some filter.
//  	"NextID"			        Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
//	}
//
// new:CDB_Set(ID) -> PLENOREFILLCOMB_TAB
// {
// 		--> CDB_Thing
//		""					// This first field MUST BE empty! (Reference)
//		""					// If not defined, use name of the two next product.
//						 	// Or directly use the IDS defined.
//      FirstProdID			// Identifier of the first product to combine or 'NO_ID' if there is no first product.
//      SecondProdID		// Identifier of the second product to combine or 'NO_ID' if there is no first product.
//		PlenoRefillID		// Identifier of the Pleno Refill group that match with this combination.
//      ""					// String to allow to apply some filter.
//  	"NextID"	        // Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
// }
//
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CTableSet(PLENOREFILLCOMB_TAB) -> ROOT_TABLE
{
	"Pleno / Pleno Refill combination"
	1						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
}

new:CDB_Set(PBA4R_REFILL) -> PLENOREFILLCOMB_TAB
{
	{
		0													// isDeleted
		1                                                   // isAvailable
		0                                                   // isHidden
		1                                                   // isFix
		0                                                   // Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation)
		0                                                   // Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
		0               									// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
	}
	""
	""
	PLENO_P_BA4_R
	NOTHING_ID			// Must be set to "NOTHING_ID" because CrossVerifyID will verify if this second ID exist in the DB or not.
	PRGROUP_P_CONNECT
	""					// String to allow to apply some filter.
	"NO_ID"			    // Identifier of the next ID to consider can be Set ID, Group ID, Product ID etc...
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////
////// Total hardness characteristic
////////////////////////////////////////////////

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_TotalHardnessCharacteristic
//
//	CDB_TotalHardnessCharacteristic help to determine the total hardness of a system.
//
//  Remark: it's not implemented as a curve but as a two dimensional array.
//
//  THL: Total Heat Load
//  VA : System Volume
//
//	new:CDB_TotalHardnessCharacteristic(ID) -> TOTALHARD_CHAR_TAB
//	{
//      Number of horizontal entries (excluding the definition of all VA ranges).
//      Number of vertical entries (It's in fact the number of VA range defined!!).
//      -1        \ -1        \ VA 1 min \ VA 1 max  \ VA 2 min \ VA 2 max  \ ...
//		THL 1 min \ THL 1 max \ �dH limit 1 for VA 1 \ �dH limit 1 for VA 2 \ ...
//		THL 2 min \ THL 2 max \ �dH limit 2 for VA 1 \ �dH limit 2 for VA 2 \ ...
//		...
//	}
//
//  Example from official documentation
//
//          Group | Total heat | System Volume | System Volume | System Volume |
//                |   load     |    limit 1    |    limit 2    |    limit 2    |
//                |   (kW)     |  < 20 l/kW    |  >= 20 l/kW   |   >= 50 l/kW  |
//                |            |               |   < 50 l/kW   |               |
//          -------------------+---------------+---------------+---------------+
//          1     | < 50       | <= 16.8 �dH   | <= 11.2 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   |
//          2     | 50-200     | <= 11.2 �dH   | <=  8.4 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   |
//          3     | 200-600    | <=  8.4 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   |
//          4     | > 600      | <= 0.11 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   | <= 0.11 �dH   |
//
//  {
//      4																// Number of horizontal entries (excluding the definition of all VA ranges).
//      3																// Number of vertical entries (It's in fact the number of VA range defined!!)
//      -1.0  \ -1.0  \ 0.00 \ 20.0 \ 20.0 \ 50.0 \ 50.0 \ -1.0			// Definition of all VA ranges.
//      0.00  \ 50.0  \ 16.8 \ 11.2 \ 0.11
//      50.0  \ 200.0 \ 11.2 \ 8.4  \ 0.11
//      200.0 \ 600.0 \ 8.4  \ 0.11 \ 0.11
//      600.0 \ -1.0  \ 0.11 \ 0.11 \ 0.11
//  }
//
//  Remark: when you define the range, put -1.0 to specify an infinite value.
//          Ex: VA 3 range = 50.0 \ -1.0   for >=50 l/kW.
//
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

// According to VDI 2035 Blatt 1.
new:CDB_TotalHardnessCharacteristic(THCHAR_VDI2014_B1) -> TOTALHARD_CHAR_TAB
{
	4																		// Number of horizontal entries (excluding the definition of all VA ranges).
	3											    						// Number of vertical entries (It's in fact the number of VA range defined!!).
	-1.0  \ -1.0  \ 0.0 \ 2.0E-05 \ 2.0E-5 \ 5.0E-5 \ 5.0E-5 \ -1.0			// VA range definitions.
	0.0   \ 5.0E4 \ 2.995720399 \ 1.997146933 \ 0.019614836					// Total heat load range min \ Total heat load range max \ total hardnesss for each VA range.
	5.0E4 \ 2.0E5 \ 1.997146933 \ 1.497860200 \ 0.019614836
	2.0E5 \ 6.0E5 \ 1.497860200 \ 0.019614836 \ 0.019614836
	6.0E5 \ -1.0  \ 0.019614836 \ 0.019614836 \ 0.019614836
}

///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//								CDB_PlenoRefill
//
//	new:CDB_PlenoRefill(ID)->tableID	Common CData syntax
//	{
//		{
//			{
//				{
//					0				isDeleted
//					1				isAvailable
//					0				isHidden
//					1				isFix
//					0				Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
//					0				Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
//      			0               Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
//				}
//				Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
//				PNRangeID			Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
//				Tmax in �C
//				Tmin in �C
//			}
//			"Reference"				Reference to the TA Product
//			"Name"					Name of the product
//			TypeID					Identifier of the valve type
//			FamilyID				Identifier of the family of the product
//			VersionID				Identifier of the version of the product
//			PriorityLevel			Level of priority for selection [1,10]
//			Comment					Product comment
//			ProdImgID				Product image ID
//			AccessGroupID			Identifier of the accessory group
//			PartOfaSet				Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
//			TableSetID				Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
//			Price					Price of the product
// 			ProductUseFlag			#eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
//			AccessorySeriesID		Identifier of the series of the accessory
//			isAttached				0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately		
//   		AccTypeID				Identifier of Accessory type if #eBoth 
//			AccFamilyID				Identifier of Accessory family if #eBoth
//		}
//		Functions			    #ePRFunc_None/#ePRFunc_Soft/#ePRFunc_Desalin
//		Capacity			    double ( l*�dH -> SI: m3*mol/m3 = mol)
//		MaxFlow				    double (m3/s)
//      MaxSupplyWaterP		    double (pa)
//      MinSupplyWaterP		    double (pa)
//		InConnectID			    string ID
//		InSizeID			    string ID
//		OutConnectID		    string ID
//		OutSizeID			    string ID
//		Height				    double (m)
//		WidthWoConnect		    double (m)
//		WidthWConnect		    double (m)
//		Weight				    double (kg)
//      DegasserCompatible		0/1 (For example: Pleno Refill 6000/12000 are not compatible with a Vento).
//
//	}
//
// Inherited Fields
//	CDB_Thing::Deleted
//	CDB_Thing::Available
//	CDB_Thing::Hidden
//	CDB_Thing::Fixed
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt1
//	CDB_Thing::FreeInt2
//	CDB_Thing::SortInt
//
//	CDB_HydroThing::Pmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::PNRange
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmax
//	CDB_HydroThing::Tmin
//
//	CDB_Product::Reference
//	CDB_Product::Name
//	CDB_Product::TypeID
//	CDB_Product::FamilyID
//	CDB_Product::VersionID
//	CDB_Product::PriorityLevel
//	CDB_Product::Comment
//	CDB_Product::ProdImgID
//	CDB_Product::AccessGroupID
//	CDB_Product::PartOfaSet
//  CDB_Product::TableSetID
//	CDB_Product::Price
//	CDB_Product::ProductUseFlag
//	CDB_Product::AccessorySeriesID
//	CDB_Product::isAttached
//	CDB_Product::AccTypeID
//	CDB_Product::AccFamilyID
//
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::Functions
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::Capacity
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::MaxFlow
//  CDB_PlenoRefill::MaxSupplyWaterP
//  CDB_PlenoRefill::MinSupplyWaterP
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::InConnectID
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::InSizeID
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::OutConnectID
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::OutSizeID
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::Height
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::WidthWoConnect
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::WidthWConnect
//	CDB_PlenoRefill::Weight
//  CDB_PlenoRefill::DegasserCompatible
///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_PlenoRefill(PR_6000) -> PLENOREFILL_TAB
{
	{
		{
			{
				0							// isDeleted
				1							// isAvailable
				0							// isHidden
				1							// isFix
				0							// Integer for flagging b31...b0 (bit 0: InCbi, bit1: available for Hub, bit2: available for HubStation )
				0							// Integer to exclude product for selection: 1 (Individual/Batch), 2 (Direct) or 4 (HMCalc).
				0               			// Sort integer (Allow to show a group of articles in the order defined with this variable).
			}
			8.0e+5 \ 8.0e+5					// Pmaxmin and Pmaxmax in Pa (if Pmaxmin = PN6, Pmaxmin is not used in PN string; a 'd' in front of Pmaxmin enforces it in PN string)
			NO_ID							// Identifier of CDB_RuledTable that contains available PN, could be NO_ID in this case Pmaxmin/max are used
			45.0	        				// Tmax in �C
			4.0             				// Tmin in �C
		}
		"813 3010"						// Reference to the Product
		"Refill 6000"					// Name of the product
		PRTYPE_MUWATER					// Identifier of the product type
		PRFAM_STD						// Identifier of the family of the product
		PRVERS_STD						// Identifier of the version of the product
		1								// Level of priority for selection [1,10]
		""								// Product comment
		"NO_ID"							// Product image ID
		ACCPRGR_6000					// Identifier of the accessory group
		#ePartOfaSetNo 					// Boolean indicating if the valve is part of a ActSet
		NO_ID							// Table ID where are sets if exist for the current product.
		0.0								// Price
		#eProduct                       // #eProduct, #eAccessory, #eBoth Integer to indicate if the Product is only Product, only Accessory or both
		NO_ID                           // Identifier of the series of the accessory (mainly used in DlgDirSel)
		0                               // 0/1: 1 if accessory cannot be ordered separately (for DlgDirSel)
		NO_ID                           // Identifier of the accessory type if #eBoth 
		NO_ID							// Identifier of the accessory family if #eBoth	
	}
	#ePRFunc_Soft					// Functions: #ePRFunc_None/#ePRFunc_Soft/#ePRFunc_Desalin
	1.069949748						// Capacity ( l/°dH -> SI: m3/mol/m3)
	6.6667e-5						// MaxFlow (m3/s)
	8.0e+5							// MaxSupplyWaterP (pa)
	2.0e+5							// MinSupplyWaterP (pa)
	CONN_SWNUT_THR					// InConnectID
	DN_20							// InSizeID
	CONN_THREADM					// OutConnectID
	DN_15							// OutSizeID
	0.571							// Height (m)
	0.275							// WidthWoConnect (m)
	0.305							// WidthWConnect (m)
	4.1								// Weight (kg)
	0								// Degasser compatible: 0/1
}

////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
//
//		Table PLENOREFILLACCGP_TAB : Pleno Refill accessory groups
//
//		Rules:
//			ACXXXID \ &ACYYYID	// ACXXXID implies ACYYYID
//			ACXXXID \ !ACYYYID	// ACXXXID excludes ACYYYID
//			>ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is built-in
//			^ACXXXID			// ACXXXID excludes all others
//		  	*ACXXXID			// ACXXXID two pieces should be included
//			#ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is distributed on each parent item (3 vessels (1 primary + 2 secondary) => 3 times the accessory).
//			+ACXXXID 			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is NOT displayed
//			++ACXXXID			// ACXXXID is an intersection between this group and an other. For this group accessory is displayed
////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////

new:CDB_RuledTable(ACCPRGR_6000) -> PLENOREFILLACCGP_TAB
{
	{
		"Pleno Refill accessories"
		0						// 0/1: 1 if this table is the true parent of the IDs in it.
	}
	PR_CART_SOFT				// 813 3101: Spare cartridge. For Pleno Refill softening module 6000/12000.
	PR_TOTALDH_MEAS				// 813 3120: Total hardness measuring. Total hardness measuring equipment for app. 100 measurements.
	PR_ELECTWATERMETER			// 813 3121: Electronic water meter. Electronic water meter with countdown function for manual make up.
	PR_ELECTWMBATT				// 813 3122: Battery for WM. Internal battery for the electronic water meter equipment.
	PR_ELECTWMPOWER				// 813 3123: External power supply for WM. External power supply for the electronic water meter equipment.
}
